2. Use `page.on('request', ...)` or `page.route(...)` to capture the POST to `api/search/events`
3. Or simply use `fetch` directly from the page context to call `api/search/events` with a constructed body (competition type "O" for Obedience, state NY, date range June 2026)

Example to try:
```js
const resp = await page.evaluate(async () => {
  const r = await fetch('/api/search/events', {method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({...})});
  return r.json();
});
```
Or intercept by adding a request listener before triggering a search via the UI, so you can see the exact payload shape.

const probes1 = await page.evaluate(() => {
  function comp(sel){
    const el=document.querySelector(sel); if(!el) return null;
    try { const p=window.ng.probe(el); const c=p&&p.componentInstance; return {sel, tag: el.tagName, compName: c&&c.constructor&&c.constructor.name, keys: c?Object.keys(c).slice(0,100):null, vals: c?Object.fromEntries(Object.keys(c).filter(k=>['searchRequest','comptype','validation','states','compEmit'].includes(k)).map(k=>[k,c[k]])):null}; } catch(e){return {sel,error:String(e)}}

const fileText2 = await fs.readFile('tmp/repl-result-DwaxjAp4rGGJuhX3.txt','utf8');
const entries2 = [];
const re2 = /- text: "((?:AB \| O \| JSHW|O)[\s\S]*?Event Approved[\s\S]*?#(\d+)[\s\S]*?)"/g;
let m2;
while ((m2 = re2.exec(fileText2))) {
  const raw = m2[1].replace(/\\n/g,'\n').replace(/\\t/g,'\t').replace(/\\"/g,'"');
  const lines = raw.split(/\n/).map(s=>s.trim()).filter(Boolean).filter(s=>!['O','AB | O | JSHW','Event Approved','Eastern Time','Opens:','Closes:','Entry Fees:','|'].includes(s));
  const date = (raw.match(/(?:Mon|Tue|Wed|Thu|Fri|Sat|Sun)\s+Jun\s+\d{2},\s+2026/)||[])[0];
  if (!date) continue;
  const eventNo = (raw.match(/#(\d+)/)||[])[1];
  const idxDate = lines.findIndex(s=>s===date);
  const club = lines[idxDate+1];
  const location = lines[idxDate+2];
  const open = (raw.match(/Opens:\s*\n\s*([^\n]+)/)||[])[1]?.trim() || '';
  const close = (raw.match(/Closes:\s*\n\s*([^\n]+)/)||[])[1]?.trim() || '';
  const types = lines[0];
  entries2.push({date, types, club, location, eventNo, open, close});
}
console.log(JSON.stringify(entries2,null,2));
console.log('count '+entries2.length);
